<table class="wikitable sortable" style="text-align:center;">
Here is the list of all Dominion card shaped items, such as events, ways, cards, ETC.

<ul><li> Most data columns indicate the card's effect on the turn when you play them (or the turn when you buy them, for <a href="/index.php/Event" title="Event">Events</a>; the turn when you receive them, for <a href="/index.php/Boon" title="Boon">Boons</a>/<a href="/index.php/Hex" title="Hex">Hexes</a>; etc). The main exception is the Victory Points: "+VP" indicate VP token wins, "VP" refer to victory card or "when scoring" effect (e.g. <a href="/index.php/Landmark" title="Landmark">Landmark</a>).
</li><li> "N" in a data column means on your next turn, "NN" means two turns from now. "N..." means on all or indefinitely many future turns.
</li><li> "C" means when you call a <a href="/index.php/Reserve" title="Reserve">Reserve</a> card.
</li><li> "?" denote a possibility (you may) or a choice on the card (e.g. <a href="/index.php/Specialist" title="Specialist">Specialist</a>).
</li><li> "!" denote a condition to get the mentioned effect by resolving the played card ("!" is not used before effect using "X" as it denote already a condition).
</li><li> Asterisks denote any other effects that relate to the card beyond the turn when it's played: "*" denotes one-shot conditions (e.g. on gain) and "**" denotes more persistent conditions (e.g. whenever another card is played).
</li><li> (Parentheses denote the likely equivalent or indirect effect of the card.)
</li><li> "P" means allowing you to play card from your hand (<a href="/index.php/Conclave" title="Conclave">Conclave</a>, <a href="/index.php/Imp" title="Imp">Imp</a>, etc.), from the supply (<a href="/index.php/Command_variant" title="Command variant">Command variants</a>) or other areas, as part of playing that card, possibly more than once (<a href="/index.php/Throne_Room_variant" title="Throne Room variant">Throne Room variants</a>). It is combined with actions/villages for Action card because it increases the number of actions you can play similarly.  It is combined with Coins/Coffer for Treasure card because it increases buying power similarly.
</li><li> "R" means <a href="/index.php/Cost_reduction" title="Cost reduction">cost reduction</a> and is combined with coins/coffers because it increases buying power similarly.
</li></ul>
<tr>
<th> Name </th>
<th> Set </th>
<th> Types </th>
<th> Cost </th>
<th> Text </th>
<th> Actions / Villagers </th>
<th> Cards </th>
<th> Buys </th>
<th> Coins / Coffers </th>
<th> Trash / Return </th>
<th> Exile </th>
<th> Junk </th>
<th> Gain </th>
<th> Victory Points
</th></tr>
